</font></td></tr></table><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><b style="font-weight:bold;">Springfield, MO, July 29, 2020</b><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"> &#8211; </font>O&#8217;Reilly Automotive, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221; or &#8220;O&#8217;Reilly&#8221;) (<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Nasdaq: &#160;</font>ORLY), a leading retailer in the automotive aftermarket industry, today announced record revenue and earnings for its second quarter ended June&#160;30,&#160;2020.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">2</font><sup style="font-size:8.25pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;vertical-align:top;">nd</sup><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"> Quarter Financial Results</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Greg Johnson, O&#8217;Reilly&#8217;s CEO and Co-President, commented, &#8220;During the second quarter and through the date of this release, the communities we serve faced significant, ongoing challenges from the COVID-19 pandemic, and our top priority continues to be the protection of the health and safety of our Team Members and customers. &#160;After experiencing significant COVID-related sales headwinds in the first two weeks of the quarter, we saw an immediate and dramatic improvement in our business and sustained robust, record-setting sales volumes throughout the remainder of our second quarter. &#160;Our DIY business was extremely strong and the bigger contributor to our 16.2% increase in comparable store sales for the quarter; however, our professional business also improved significantly as we progressed through the quarter, generating robust comparable store sales above our expectations in May and June. &#160;It is clear there were several positive macroeconomic factors that supported the strong demand in our industry in the second quarter, including, among others, the government stimulus and unemployment benefits and the re-opening of consumer activity as stay-at-home orders began lifting. &#160;As beneficial as the market conditions were in the second quarter, we know our record-setting financial performance would not have been possible without outstanding execution by our dedicated, hard-working Team. &#160;We are extremely proud of the outstanding job our Team has done to implement safety measures while still providing the outstanding service that has been so critical to our customers during this pandemic.&#8221;</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="font-size:10pt;visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Mr. Johnson further commented, &#8220;Our Team&#8217;s performance in the second quarter is even more impressive in light of the cost control steps we executed to conserve cash and align our business with the severe headwinds we were experiencing at the beginning of the second quarter. &#160;We were very pleased to see our business rebound, as our customers began to benefit under the CARES Act in the middle of April, but we maintained a prudent, cautious approach as we progressed through the second quarter, taking into consideration the high level of uncertainty regarding how our business would perform week to week. &#160;The combination of strong sales and strong expense control resulted in an incredible operating profit margin of 23.8% during the second quarter, which exceeds our previous best single quarter performance by well over 300 basis points. &#160;While we recognize this remarkably strong leverage of SG&amp;A expense is not sustainable over the long term and expect our per-store dollar spend to increase as we continually match service levels to the business environment, our Team&#8217;s ability to deliver such an outstanding quarter is an incredible accomplishment, and we want to offer our sincere thanks to Team O&#8217;Reilly for their selfless dedication to our customers.&#8221;</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Sales for the second quarter ended June&#160;30,&#160;2020, increased $502 million, or 19%, to $3.09 billion from $2.59 billion for the same period one year ago. &#160;Gross profit for the second quarter increased 20% to $1.64 billion (or 53.0% of sales) from $1.37 billion (or 52.8% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Selling, general and administrative expenses (&#8220;SG&amp;A&#8221;) for the second quarter increased 4% to $901 million (or 29.1% of sales) from $870 million (or 33.6% of sales) for the same </p></div><div style="clear:both;margin-bottom:30pt;width:100%;"><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:center;margin:24pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p></div></div><hr style="background-color:#000000;clear:both;color:#000000;height:2pt;line-height:0;margin-bottom:30pt;margin-left:5.88%;margin-right:5.88%;margin-top:30pt;page-break-after:always;width:88.24%;border-width:0;"><div style="max-width:100%;padding-left:5.88%;padding-right:5.88%;position:relative;"><div style="clear:both;max-width:100%;position:relative;"><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">period one year ago. &#160;Operating income for the second quarter increased 48% to $736 million (or 23.8% of sales) from $498 million (or 19.2% of sales) for the same period one year ago. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Net income for the second quarter ended June&#160;30,&#160;2020, increased $178 million, or 50%, to $532 million (or 17.2% of sales) from $354 million (or 13.7% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Diluted earnings per common share for the second quarter increased 57% to $7.10 on 75 million shares versus $4.51 on 78 million shares for the same period one year ago. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Year-to-Date Financial Results</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Sales for the first six months of 2020 increased $568 million, or 11%, to $5.57 billion from $5.00 billion for the same period one year ago. &#160;Gross profit for the first six months of 2020 increased 11% to $2.93 billion (or 52.7% of sales) from $2.65 billion (or 52.9% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;SG&amp;A for the first six months of 2020 increased 4% to $1.77 billion (or 31.8% of sales) from $1.70 billion (or 34.1% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Operating income for the first six months of 2020 increased 23% to $1.16 billion (or 20.8% of sales) from $943 million (or 18.9% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Net income for the first six months of 2020 increased $157 million, or 23%, to $832 million (or 14.9% of sales) from $675 million (or 13.5% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Diluted earnings per common share for the first six months of 2020 increased 29% to $11.06 on 75 million shares versus $8.56 on 79 million shares for the same period one year ago. &#160;</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">2</font><sup style="font-size:8.25pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;vertical-align:top;">nd</sup><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"> Quarter Comparable Store Sales Results</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Comparable store sales are calculated based on the change in sales for U.S. stores open at least one year and exclude sales of specialty machinery, sales to independent parts stores and sales to Team Members, as well as sales from Leap Day in the six months ended June 30, 2020. &#160;Online sales, resulting from ship-to-home orders and pick-up-in-store orders, for U.S. stores open at least one year, are included in the comparable store sales calculation. &#160;Comparable store sales increased 16.2% for the second quarter ended June&#160;30,&#160;2020, on top of 3.4% for the same period one year ago. &#160;Comparable store sales increased 7.5% for the six months ended June&#160;30,&#160;2020, on top of 3.3% for the same period one year ago. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Share Repurchase Program</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">In order to conserve liquidity in response to COVID-19, the Company suspended its share repurchase program on March 16, 2020. &#160;The Company continued to evaluate business conditions and its liquidity and, as a result of this evaluation, resumed its share repurchase program on May 29, 2020. &#160;During the second quarter ended June&#160;30,&#160;2020, the Company repurchased 0.2 million shares of its common stock, at an average price per share of $417.79, for a total investment of $77 million. &#160;During the first six months ended of 2020, the Company repurchased 1.7 million shares of its common stock, at an average price per share of $390.14, for a total investment of $651 million. &#160;Subsequent to the end of the second quarter and through the date of this release, the Company repurchased an additional 0.1 million shares of its common stock, at an average price per share of $423.09, for a total investment of $36 million. &#160;The Company has repurchased a total of 77.9 million shares of its common stock under its share repurchase program since the inception of the program in January of 2011 and through the date of this release, at an average price of $165.10, for a total aggregate investment of $12.87 billion. &#160;As of the date of this release, the Company had approximately $882 million remaining under its current share repurchase authorization. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Continued Suspension of 2020 Guidance</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">As previously announced, the Company withdrew all previously issued 2020 guidance, and given the ongoing uncertainty related to COVID-19, the Company is not resuming 2020 guidance at this time. &#160;</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Non-GAAP Information</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">This release contains certain financial information not derived in accordance with United States generally accepted accounting principles (&#8220;GAAP&#8221;). &#160;These items include adjusted debt to earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation, amortization, share-based compensation and rent (&#8220;EBITDAR&#8221;) and free cash flow. &#160;The Company does not, nor does it suggest investors should, consider such non-GAAP financial measures in isolation from, or as a substitute for, GAAP financial information. &#160;The Company believes that the presentation of adjusted debt to EBITDAR and free cash flow provide meaningful supplemental information to both management and investors that is indicative of the Company&#8217;s core operations. &#160;</p></div><div style="clear:both;margin-bottom:30pt;width:100%;"><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:center;margin:24pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p></div></div><hr financial information below. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p Information</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">The Company will host a conference call on Thursday, July 30, 2020, at 10:00 a.m. Central Time to discuss its results as well as future expectations. &#160;Investors may listen to the conference call live on the Company&#8217;s website at <u style="text-decoration:underline;text-decoration-color:#000000;">www.OReillyAuto.com</u> by clicking on &#8220;Investor Relations&#8221; and then &#8220;News Room.&#8221; &#160;Interested analysts are invited to join the call. &#160;The dial-in number for the call is (703) 375-5524; the conference call identification number is 8265809. &#160;A replay of the conference call will be available on the Company&#8217;s website through Thursday, July 29, 2021. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">About O&#8217;Reilly Automotive, Inc.</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">O&#8217;Reilly Automotive, Inc. was founded in 1957 by the O&#8217;Reilly family and is one of the largest specialty retailers of automotive aftermarket parts, tools, supplies, equipment and accessories in the United States, serving both the do-it-yourself and professional service provider markets. &#160;Visit the Company&#8217;s website at <u style="text-decoration:underline;text-decoration-color:#000000;">www.OReillyAuto.com</u> for additional information about O&#8217;Reilly, including access to online shopping and current promotions, store locations, hours and services, employment opportunities and other programs. &#160;As of June&#160;30,&#160;2020, the Company operated 5,562 stores in 47 U.S. states and 21 stores in Mexico. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Forward-Looking
